     <li class="b_algo">
      <h2>
       <a h="ID=SERP,5186.1" href="https://www.programiz.com/c-programming/examples/print-sentence" target="_blank">
        C "Hello, World!" Program
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="b_caption">
       <div class="b_attribution" u="1|5065|4599747071382966|ofWc-q9RMKYruXa8wShzjikkfnqq56RB">
        <cite>
         https://www.programiz.com/c-programming/examples/print-sentence
        </cite>
        <span class="c_tlbxTrg">
         <span class="c_tlbxH" h="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" k="SERP,5187.1">
         </span>
        </span>
       </div>
       <p>
        How "Hello,
        <strong>
        </strong>
        World!" program works? The #include is a preprocessor command that tells the compiler to include the contents of stdio.h (standard input and output) file in the program.; The stdio.h file contains functions such as scanf() and printf() to take input and display output respectively.; If you use the printf() function without writing #include &lt;stdio.h&gt;, the program will 
       </p>
      </div>
     </li>
     <li class="b_algo">
      <div class="b_title">
       <h2>
        <a h="ID=SERP,5209.1" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%22Hello,_World!%22_program" target="_blank">

        </a>
       </h2>

         <span aria-label="Show more" class="scs_arw" tabindex="0">
         </span>
        </a>

         <div class="tab-content">
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_10_150741_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5486.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_10_150741" role="tabpanel">
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_11_15080A_head" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5487.2" data-priority="" id="tab_11_15080A" role="tabpanel">
           <p class="b_paractl">
            "Time to hello world" (TTHW) is the time it takes to author a "Hello, World!" program in a given programming language. This is one measure of a programming language's ease-of-use; since the program is meant as an introduction for people unfamiliar with the language, a more complex "Hello, World!" program may indicate that the programming language is less approachable.  The concept has been extended beyond programming languages to APIs, as a measure of how simp
           </p>
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_12_1509E1_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5488.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_12_1509E1" role="tabpanel">
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_13_150A58_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5489.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_13_150A58" role="tabpanel">
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_14_150AB0_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5490.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_14_150AB0" role="tabpanel">
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_15_150B03_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5491.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_15_150B03" role="tabpanel">
          </div>
          <div aria-labelledby="tab_16_150B53_head" class="tab-hide" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5492.2" data-priority="2" id="tab_16_150B53" role="tabpanel">

             <li data-priority="">
              <div>
               There are different headers in C++,
               <strong>
                each of which contain information that is necessary in the program.
                <strong>
                </strong>
                The
               </strong>
               header
               <strong>
                is used in this program which provides basic input and output services for
               </strong>
               C++
               <strong>
                programs.
               </strong>
              </div>

     <li class="b_algo">
      <h2>
       <a h="ID=SERP,5247.1" href="https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/hello-world-in-c-sharp/" target="_blank">
        Hello World in C# - GeeksforGeeks
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="b_caption">
       <div class="b_attribution" u="4|5068|4570996558072947|zdSESTkWWwcepkBuGhDJJZ4oO4fwrDwR">
        <cite>
         https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/
         <strong>
          hello-world-in
         </strong>
         -c-sharp
        </cite>
        <span class="c_tlbxTrg">
         <span class="c_tlbxH" h="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" k="SERP,5248.1">
         </span>
        </span>
       </div>
       <p>
        <span class="news_dt">
         10/10/2018
        </span>
         The Hello World! program is the most basic and first program when you dive into a new programming language. This simply prints the Hello World! on the output screen. In C#, a basic program consists of the following: A Namespace Declaration; Class Declaration &amp; Definition; Class Members(like variables, methods etc.) Main Method; Statements or Expressions. 
       </p>
       <div class="b_factrow b_twofr">
        <div class="b_vlist2col">
         <ul>
          <li>
           <div>
            <strong>
             Estimated Reading Time:
            </strong>
            3 mins
           </div>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <ul>
         </ul>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>

     <li class="b_algo">
      <h2>
       <a h="ID=SERP,5263.1" href="https://www.tutorialspoint.com/Hello-World-Program-in-Java" target="_blank">
        Hello World Program in Java - Tutorialspoint
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="b_caption">
       <div class="b_attribution" u="5|5069|5066502640502883|6uforVI0jdb_-uEUtYtED0gnuy4cIoZ1">
        <cite>
         https://
         <strong>
          www.tutorialspoint.com
         </strong>
         /
         <strong>
          Hello-World-Program-in-Java
         </strong>
        </cite>
        <span class="c_tlbxTrg">
         <span class="c_tlbxH" h="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" k="SERP,5264.1">
         </span>
        </span>
       </div>
       <p>
        <span class="news_dt">
         19/01/2018
        </span>
         Type 'javac MyFirstJavaProgram.java' and press enter to compile your code. If there are no errors in your code, the command prompt will take you to the next line (Assumption  The path variable is set). Now, type ' java MyFirstJavaProgram ' to run your program. You will be able to see ' Hello World ' printed on the window.
       </p>

              <div>
               <span data-translation="" id="dscexpitem_-1644579518_49">
                <span data-translation="" id="KCA1_48">
                 Hello World, stylized as HELLO WORLD, is a 2019 Japanese animated science fiction romantic drama film directed by Tomohiko It from an original screenplay written by Mado Nozaki. Produce
                </span>
                <div class="sml inline" data-appns="SERP" data-expl="" data-k="5706.1" id="expitem_-1644579518_49">
                 <a aria-describedby="expansionAccessibilityTextexpitem_-1644579518_49_hit" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Show more" class="b_mopexpref" data-exp="I;expitem_-1644579518_49;;0;;KCA1_48;KCTaskpane;KCA1TextExpand;0;0;expitem_-1644579518_49_hit;10;0" href="javascript:void(0);" id="expitem_-1644579518_49_hit" role="button">
                  <span class="sw_plus cipa" height="16" width="16">
                  </span>
                  <div class="expansionAccessibilityText" id="expansionAccessibilityTextexpitem_-1644579518_49_hit">
                   New content will be added above the current area of focus upon selection
                  </div>
                 </a>
                </div>
               </span>
               <div class="b_hide" data-exp="H;expitem_-1644579518_49;;dscexpitem_-1644579518_49;;;" data-exp-noani="">
                <span data-translation="">
                 Hello World, stylized as HELLO WORLD, is a 2019 Japanese animated science fiction romantic drama film directed by Tomohiko It from an original screenplay written by Mado Nozaki. Produced by Graphinica, the film is set in a futuristic Kyoto where a high school student named Naomi Katagaki encounters a person claiming to be himself, who time-traveled from 10 years in the future to save a classmate named Ruri Ichigy.
                </span>
